 The Supreme Court has removed 2 court officials from the post for tampering with the uploaded judicial verdict
 in donon adhikariyon par galati se udyogpati anil ambani ke court kii avmaananaa se jude ek maamle main court main nijee taur par upasthit rahane ko chhot pradaan karne kaa aarope he
 The country's largest court removed 2 masters of the court, exercising higher authority under Section 311 of the Constitution

 iske alaava anya karkon se bhi maang prabhavit hui
